## Diff

- NEW web/components/citation/citation_chip.tsx: base-ui Tooltip (hover+focus+touch+Esc), chip = tier-dot (--tier-1/2/3) + mono id/index, min 24px target, focus-visible ring /70; source card shows EXACT untruncated quote (max-h scroll) OR honest "span not renderable" fallback; Canada-red --primary url link.

## Review focus (rubric: provability/honesty, a11y, visual, code)

 succeeded in 1083ms:
   1: // I-p2-004 (#743): the SINGLE shared resolver for provenance-token → exact
   2: // source span. Consumed by the citation chip now and by the Proof-Replay
   3: // inspector (#756) — one resolver boundary, no duplicate parsing.
   4: //
   5: // No-synthetic-proof contract (Codex brief iter-2/3): returns quote=null
   6: // (→ honest fallback) unless the bounds are fully valid against the actual
   7: // source body. NEVER a silently-clamped slice (that would be synthetic proof).
   8: 
   9: import { parseProvenanceToken } from "@/lib/provenance_tokens";
  10: 
  11: export interface EvidenceSource {
  12:   source_id: string;
  13:   full_text?: string | null;
  14:   snippet?: string | null;
  15:   title?: string | null;
  16:   url?: string | null;
  17:   tier?: string | number | null;
  18: }
  19: 
  20: export interface ResolvedSpan {
  21:   raw: string;
  22:   sourceId: string;
  23:   source: EvidenceSource | null;
  24:   start: number;
  25:   end: number;
  26:   /** The EXACT cited passage `full_text[start:end]`, or null when unresolved
  27:    * (missing source / no full_text / out-of-range bounds) — never clamped. */
  28:   quote: string | null;
  29: }
  30: 
  31: function sourcesOf(evidencePool: unknown): EvidenceSource[] {
  32:   const s = (evidencePool as { sources?: unknown } | null)?.sources;
  33:   return Array.isArray(s) ? (s as EvidenceSource[]) : [];
  34: }
  35: 
  36: /** Resolve a `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` token against the evidence pool.
  37:  * Returns null if the token itself is malformed; otherwise a ResolvedSpan
  38:  * whose `quote` is null unless every bound is valid against the real body. */
  39: export function resolveSpan(
  40:   token: string,
  41:   evidencePool: unknown,
  42: ): ResolvedSpan | null {
  43:   const parsed = parseProvenanceToken(token);
  44:   if (!parsed) return null;
  45:   // sources is an ARRAY → look up by source_id (never index).
  46:   const source =
  47:     sourcesOf(evidencePool).find((s) => s?.source_id === parsed.source_id) ??
  48:     null;
  49:   const body = source?.full_text ?? null; // exact span only from full_text
  50:   let quote: string | null = null;
  51:   if (
  52:     typeof body === "string" &&
  53:     body.length > 0 &&
  54:     parsed.start >= 0 &&
  55:     parsed.end <= body.length &&
  56:     parsed.start <= parsed.end
  57:   ) {
  58:     quote = body.slice(parsed.start, parsed.end);
  59:   }
  60:   return {
  61:     raw: token,
  62:     sourceId: parsed.source_id,
  63:     source,
  64:     start: parsed.start,
  65:     end: parsed.end,
  66:     quote,
  67:   };
  68: }

 succeeded in 1323ms:
   1: // I-f5-003 — frontend mirror of polaris_graph.generator2.provenance.
   2: 
   3: const TOKEN_RE = /^\[#ev:([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+):(\d+)-(\d+)\]$/;
   4: 
   5: export interface ParsedToken {
   6:   raw: string;
   7:   source_id: string;
   8:   start: number;
   9:   end: number;
  10: }
  11: 
  12: export function parseProvenanceToken(token: string): ParsedToken | null {
  13:   const match = TOKEN_RE.exec(token.trim());
  14:   if (!match) return null;
  15:   return {
  16:     raw: token,
  17:     source_id: match[1],
  18:     start: parseInt(match[2], 10),
  19:     end: parseInt(match[3], 10),
  20:   };
  21: }
  22: 
  23: export function parseAllTokens(tokens: string[]): ParsedToken[] {
  24:   return tokens
  25:     .map(parseProvenanceToken)
  26:     .filter((t): t is ParsedToken => t !== null);
  27: }

   1: "use client";

   3: import { Tooltip } from "@base-ui/react/tooltip";
   4: import * as React from "react";
   5: 
   6: interface EvidenceTooltipProps {
   7:   evidenceId: string;
   8:   sourceUrl?: string;
   9:   spanText?: string;
  10:   sourceTier?: string;
  11:   /**
  12:    * I-f6-001: optional publication-date string surfaced in the popup
  13:    * as `Published: <date>`. When undefined/null, the line is omitted.
  14:    */
  15:   publishedDate?: string | null;
  16:   /**
  17:    * I-f6-002: requested popup side. Default "top" (back-compat). Base UI
  18:    * Positioner applies flip+shift collision avoidance automatically when
  19:    * the requested side would clip the viewport.
  20:    */
  21:   side?: "top" | "right" | "bottom" | "left";
  22:   /**
  23:    * I-f6-005: opt-in perf-test override. When defined, drives Tooltip.Root's
  24:    * `open` directly, bypassing the internal hover/focus/touch state machine.
  25:    * Default `undefined` → no behavior change for existing callers.
  26:    */
  27:   openOverride?: boolean;
  28:   onClickToInspect?: () => void;
  29:   children: React.ReactNode;
  30: }
  31: 
  32: const HOVER_DEBOUNCE_MS = 300;
  33: const TOUCH_AUTO_CLOSE_MS = 3000;
  34: 
  35: /**
  36:  * F6 citation overlay (Phase 2B Task 2B.1) — hover-card preview of the
  37:  * source span behind a provenance token. Click still triggers the right-
  38:  * pane Inspector view; hover shows a quick preview.
  39:  *
  40:  * I-f6-003: fully-controlled Tooltip with explicit hover/focus/touch open
  41:  * semantics. Touch tap opens the popup with a 3-second auto-close timer
  42:  * (Base UI's `closeOnClick={false}` prevents the referencePress dismiss
  43:  * from cancelling our touch-open in the same event).
  44:  */
  45: export function EvidenceTooltip({
  46:   evidenceId,
  47:   sourceUrl,
  48:   spanText,
  49:   sourceTier,
  50:   publishedDate,
  51:   side = "top",
  52:   openOverride,
  53:   onClickToInspect,
  54:   children,
  55: }: EvidenceTooltipProps) {
  56:   const [open, setOpen] = React.useState(false);
  57:   const hoverDebounceRef = React.useRef<number | null>(null);
  58:   const touchAutoCloseRef = React.useRef<number | null>(null);
  59:   const touchSessionRef = React.useRef(false);
  60: 
  61:   const clearHoverDebounce = React.useCallback(() => {
  62:     if (hoverDebounceRef.current !== null) {
  63:       window.clearTimeout(hoverDebounceRef.current);
  64:       hoverDebounceRef.current = null;
  65:     }
  66:   }, []);
  67: 
  68:   const clearTouchAutoClose = React.useCallback(() => {
  69:     if (touchAutoCloseRef.current !== null) {
  70:       window.clearTimeout(touchAutoCloseRef.current);
  71:       touchAutoCloseRef.current = null;
  72:     }
  73:   }, []);
  74: 
  75:   const handleOpenChange = React.useCallback(
  76:     (next: boolean) => {
  77:       if (!next) {
  78:         clearHoverDebounce();
  79:         clearTouchAutoClose();
  80:         touchSessionRef.current = false;
  81:       }
  82:       setOpen(next);
  83:     },
  84:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
  85:   );
  86: 
  87:   React.useEffect(
  88:     () => () => {
  89:       clearHoverDebounce();
  90:       clearTouchAutoClose();
  91:     },
  92:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
  93:   );
  94: 
  95:   const handleMouseEnter = React.useCallback(() => {
  96:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
  97:     clearHoverDebounce();
  98:     hoverDebounceRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
  99:       hoverDebounceRef.current = null;
 100:       setOpen(true);
 101:     }, HOVER_DEBOUNCE_MS);
 102:   }, [clearHoverDebounce]);
 103: 
 104:   const handleMouseLeave = React.useCallback(() => {
 105:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 106:     clearHoverDebounce();
 107:     setOpen(false);
 108:   }, [clearHoverDebounce]);
 109: 
 110:   const handleFocus = React.useCallback(() => {
 111:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 112:     setOpen(true);
 113:   }, []);
 114: 
 115:   const handleBlur = React.useCallback(() => {
 116:     if (touchSessionRef.current) return;
 117:     setOpen(false);
 118:   }, []);
 119: 
 120:   const handlePointerDown = React.useCallback(
 121:     (event: React.PointerEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
 122:       if (event.pointerType !== "touch") return;
 123:       touchSessionRef.current = true;
 124:       clearHoverDebounce();
 125:       clearTouchAutoClose();
 126:       setOpen(true);
 127:       touchAutoCloseRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
 128:         touchAutoCloseRef.current = null;
 129:         touchSessionRef.current = false;
 130:         setOpen(false);
 131:       }, TOUCH_AUTO_CLOSE_MS);
 132:     },
 133:     [clearHoverDebounce, clearTouchAutoClose],
 134:   );
 135: 
 136:   const final_open = openOverride ?? open;
 137:   return (
 138:     <Tooltip.Root open={final_open} onOpenChange={handleOpenChange}>
 139:       <Tooltip.Trigger
 140:         closeOnClick={false}
 141:         render={
 142:           <button
 143:             type="button"
 144:             onClick={onClickToInspect}
 145:             onMouseEnter={handleMouseEnter}
 146:             onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
 147:             onFocus={handleFocus}
 148:             onBlur={handleBlur}
 149:             onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
 150:             className="text-foreground bg-muted hover:bg-foreground hover:text-background mx-0.5 inline-flex min-h-[24px] cursor-pointer items-center rounded px-1.5 py-0.5 font-mono text-xs transition"
 151:           />
 152:         }
 153:       >
 154:         {children}
 155:       </Tooltip.Trigger>
 156:       <Tooltip.Portal>
 157:         <Tooltip.Positioner sideOffset={6} side={side}>
 158:           <Tooltip.Popup
 159:             data-testid="evidence-tooltip-popup"
 160:             className="border-border bg-background text-foreground z-50 max-w-md rounded-md border p-3 shadow-md"
 161:           >
 162:             <p className="text-muted-foreground font-mono text-[11px]">
 163:               {evidenceId}
 164:               {sourceTier && ` · tier ${sourceTier}`}
 165:             </p>
 166:             {sourceUrl && (
 167:               <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-1 truncate text-[11px]">
 168:                 {sourceUrl}
 169:               </p>
 170:             )}
 171:             {publishedDate && (
 172:               <p
 173:                 data-testid="evidence-tooltip-published"
 174:                 className="text-muted-foreground mt-1 text-[11px]"
 175:               >
 176:                 Published: {publishedDate}
 177:               </p>
 178:             )}
 179:             {spanText && (
 180:               <p className="text-foreground mt-2 text-xs leading-snug">
 181:                 &ldquo;
 182:                 {spanText.length > 240
 183:                   ? spanText.slice(0, 240) + "…"
 184:                   : spanText}
 185:                 &rdquo;
 186:               </p>
 187:             )}
 188:             <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-2 text-[11px] italic">
 189:               Click to pin in Evidence pane
 190:             </p>
 191:           </Tooltip.Popup>
 192:         </Tooltip.Positioner>
 193:       </Tooltip.Portal>
 194:     </Tooltip.Root>
 195:   );
 196: }

 succeeded in 1980ms:
   1: // I-p2-004 (#743): reusable citation chip + hover/focus source card.
   2: // Chip = inline provenance marker (tier dot + mono index/id). Hover OR focus OR
   3: // tap → source card with the EXACT cited span (untruncated) via resolveSpan.
   4: // No-synthetic-proof: shows the span only when resolved, else an honest note.
   5: "use client";
   6: 
   7: import { Tooltip } from "@base-ui/react/tooltip";
   8: import { useState } from "react";
   9: 
  10: import { resolveSpan } from "@/lib/evidence_span";
  11: 
  12: interface CitationChipProps {
  13:   /** A provenance token `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]`. */
  14:   token: string;
  15:   /** The run's evidence pool (EvidenceContract / bundle.evidencePool). */
  16:   evidencePool: unknown;
  17:   /** Optional display index (e.g. the nth citation in a sentence). */
  18:   index?: number;
  19: }
  20: 
  21: function tierDotClass(tier: string | number | null | undefined): string {
  22:   const t = String(tier ?? "").toUpperCase();
  23:   if (t === "T1" || t === "1") return "bg-tier-1"; // primary evidence (red)
  24:   if (t === "T2" || t === "2") return "bg-tier-2";
  25:   return "bg-tier-3";
  26: }
  27: 
  28: export function CitationChip({
  29:   token,
  30:   evidencePool,
  31:   index,
  32: }: CitationChipProps) {
  33:   const span = resolveSpan(token, evidencePool);
  34:   const tier = span?.source?.tier ?? null;
  35:   const label = span?.source?.title ?? span?.sourceId ?? token;
  36:   // Controlled open so hover (mouse), focus (keyboard) AND tap (touch) all open
  37:   // the source card — base-ui hover alone is mouse-only (Codex iter-1 P1).
  38:   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  39: 
  40:   return (
  41:     <Tooltip.Root open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
  42:       <Tooltip.Trigger
  43:         closeOnClick={false}
  44:         render={
  45:           <button
  46:             type="button"
  47:             data-testid="citation-chip"
  48:             data-source-id={span?.sourceId}
  49:             aria-label={`Source: ${label}`}
  50:             onClick={() => setOpen((o) => !o)}
  51:             onMouseEnter={() => setOpen(true)}
  52:             onMouseLeave={() => setOpen(false)}
  53:             onFocus={() => setOpen(true)}
  54:             onBlur={() => setOpen(false)}
  55:             className="border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted focus-visible:ring-ring/70 mx-0.5 inline-flex min-h-[24px] min-w-[24px] items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded border px-1.5 align-baseline font-mono text-[11px] leading-none transition-colors focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:outline-none"
  56:           />
  57:         }
  58:       >
  59:         <span
  60:           aria-hidden
  61:           className={`inline-block h-1.5 w-1.5 shrink-0 rounded-full ${tierDotClass(tier)}`}
  62:         />
  63:         {index != null ? index : (span?.sourceId ?? "ev")}
  64:       </Tooltip.Trigger>
  65:       <Tooltip.Portal>
  66:         <Tooltip.Positioner sideOffset={6}>
  67:           <Tooltip.Popup
  68:             data-testid="citation-source-card"
  69:             className="border-border bg-background text-foreground z-50 max-w-md rounded-md border p-3 shadow-md"
  70:           >
  71:             <div className="text-muted-foreground mb-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 text-[11px]">
  72:               <span className="text-foreground font-medium">{label}</span>
  73:               {tier != null && <span>· tier {String(tier)}</span>}
  74:               <span className="font-mono">
  75:                 [{span?.sourceId ?? "?"}:{span?.start ?? "?"}-{span?.end ?? "?"}
  76:                 ]
  77:               </span>
  78:             </div>
  79:             {span?.quote != null ? (
  80:               <blockquote className="text-foreground border-border max-h-48 overflow-auto border-l-2 pl-3 text-xs leading-snug italic">
  81:                 &ldquo;{span.quote}&rdquo;
  82:               </blockquote>
  83:             ) : (
  84:               <p className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">
  85:                 Source span not renderable from this bundle — verify via the
  86:                 signed bundle.
  87:               </p>
  88:             )}
  89:             {span?.source?.url && (
  90:               <a
  91:                 href={span.source.url}
  92:                 target="_blank"
  93:                 rel="noopener noreferrer"
  94:                 className="text-primary mt-1 block max-w-full truncate text-[11px] underline-offset-2 hover:underline"
  95:               >
  96:                 {span.source.url}
  97:               </a>
  98:             )}
  99:           </Tooltip.Popup>
 100:         </Tooltip.Positioner>
 101:       </Tooltip.Portal>
 102:     </Tooltip.Root>
 103:   );
 104: }

  27: +function tierDotClass(tier: string | number | null | undefined): string {
  28: +  const t = String(tier ?? "").toUpperCase();
  29: +  if (t === "T1" || t === "1") return "bg-tier-1"; // primary evidence (red)
  30: +  if (t === "T2" || t === "2") return "bg-tier-2";
  31: +  return "bg-tier-3";
  32: +}
  33: +
  34: +export function CitationChip({
  35: +  token,
  36: +  evidencePool,
  37: +  index,
  38: +}: CitationChipProps) {

 111: diff --git a/web/lib/evidence_span.ts b/web/lib/evidence_span.ts
 112: new file mode 100644
 113: index 00000000..71b58e0c
 114: --- /dev/null
 115: +++ b/web/lib/evidence_span.ts
 116: @@ -0,0 +1,68 @@
 117: +// I-p2-004 (#743): the SINGLE shared resolver for provenance-token → exact
 118: +// source span. Consumed by the citation chip now and by the Proof-Replay
 119: +// inspector (#756) — one resolver boundary, no duplicate parsing.
 120: +//
 121: +// No-synthetic-proof contract (Codex brief iter-2/3): returns quote=null
 122: +// (→ honest fallback) unless the bounds are fully valid against the actual
 123: +// source body. NEVER a silently-clamped slice (that would be synthetic proof).
 124: +
 125: +import { parseProvenanceToken } from "@/lib/provenance_tokens";
 126: +
 127: +export interface EvidenceSource {
 128: +  source_id: string;
 129: +  full_text?: string | null;
 130: +  snippet?: string | null;
 131: +  title?: string | null;
 132: +  url?: string | null;
 133: +  tier?: string | number | null;
 134: +}
 135: +
 136: +export interface ResolvedSpan {
 137: +  raw: string;
 138: +  sourceId: string;
 139: +  source: EvidenceSource | null;
 140: +  start: number;
 141: +  end: number;
 142: +  /** The EXACT cited passage `full_text[start:end]`, or null when unresolved
 143: +   * (missing source / no full_text / out-of-range bounds) — never clamped. */
 144: +  quote: string | null;
 145: +}
 146: +
 147: +function sourcesOf(evidencePool: unknown): EvidenceSource[] {
 148: +  const s = (evidencePool as { sources?: unknown } | null)?.sources;
 149: +  return Array.isArray(s) ? (s as EvidenceSource[]) : [];
 150: +}
 151: +
 152: +/** Resolve a `[#ev:<id>:<start>-<end>]` token against the evidence pool.
 153: + * Returns null if the token itself is malformed; otherwise a ResolvedSpan
 154: + * whose `quote` is null unless every bound is valid against the real body. */
 155: +export function resolveSpan(
 156: +  token: string,
 157: +  evidencePool: unknown,
 158: +): ResolvedSpan | null {
 159: +  const parsed = parseProvenanceToken(token);
 160: +  if (!parsed) return null;
 161: +  // sources is an ARRAY → look up by source_id (never index).
 162: +  const source =
 163: +    sourcesOf(evidencePool).find((s) => s?.source_id === parsed.source_id) ??
 164: +    null;
 165: +  const body = source?.full_text ?? null; // exact span only from full_text
 166: +  let quote: string | null = null;
 167: +  if (
 168: +    typeof body === "string" &&
 169: +    body.length > 0 &&
 170: +    parsed.start >= 0 &&
 171: +    parsed.end <= body.length &&
 172: +    parsed.start <= parsed.end
 173: +  ) {
 174: +    quote = body.slice(parsed.start, parsed.end);
 175: +  }
 176: +  return {
 177: +    raw: token,
 178: +    sourceId: parsed.source_id,
 179: +    source,
 180: +    start: parsed.start,
 181: +    end: parsed.end,
 182: +    quote,
 183: +  };
 184: +}

 720: export interface RetrievalErrorBody {
 721:   error: true;
 722:   code: "wrong_status" | "wrong_scope_class" | "fetch_backend_unavailable";
 723:   message: string;
 724:   decision_id: string | null;
 725: }
 726: 
 727: export class RetrievalBadRequestError extends Error {
 728:   code: RetrievalErrorBody["code"];
 729:   decision_id: string | null;
 730:   constructor(body: RetrievalErrorBody) {
 731:     super(body.message);
 732:     this.name = "RetrievalBadRequestError";
 733:     this.code = body.code;
 734:     this.decision_id = body.decision_id;
 735:   }
 736: }
 737: 
 738: export async function runRetrieval(
 739:   decision: IntakeScopeDecision,
 740: ): Promise<RetrievalSuccessResponse> {
 741:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/api/retrieval`, {
 742:     method: "POST",
 743:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 744:     body: JSON.stringify({ decision }),
 745:   });
 746: 
 747:   if (response.status === 400) {
 748:     const detail = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 749:     const body = (detail?.detail ?? detail) as RetrievalErrorBody | null;
 750:     if (body && body.error) {
 751:       throw new RetrievalBadRequestError(body);
 752:     }
 753:   }
 754: 
 755:   return asJsonOrThrow<RetrievalSuccessResponse>(response);
 756: }
 757:

 770: /** Convenience: count sources matching a given tier. */
 771: export function countSourcesByTier(
 772:   pool: EvidencePool,
 773:   tier: RetrievalSourceTier,
 774: ): number {
 775:   return pool.sources.filter((s) => s.tier === tier).length;
 776: }
 777: 
 778: /** Convenience: dedupe + sort sources by tier (T1 first), then by domain. */
 779: export function sortSourcesByTier(
 780:   sources: RetrievalSource[],
 781: ): RetrievalSource[] {
 782:   const tier_rank: Record<RetrievalSourceTier, number> = {
 783:     T1: 0,
 784:     T2: 1,
 785:     T3: 2,
 786:   };
 787:   return [...sources].sort((a, b) => {
 788:     const t = tier_rank[a.tier] - tier_rank[b.tier];
 789:     if (t !== 0) return t;
 790:     return a.domain.localeCompare(b.domain);
 791:   });
 792: }

 231:   sentence,
 232:   sentence_id,
 233:   pool,
 234: }: {
 235:   open: boolean;
 236:   onOpenChange: (next: boolean) => void;

 238:   sentence_id: string | null;

 244:   for (const tok of tokens) {
 245:     const arr = grouped.get(tok.source_id) ?? [];
 246:     arr.push(tok);
 247:     grouped.set(tok.source_id, arr);
 248:   }
 249:   const groups = [...grouped.entries()];

   8: import { useIsoLayoutEffect } from '@base-ui/utils/useIsoLayoutEffect';

  15: import { useFloatingParentNodeId, useFloatingTree } from "../components/FloatingTree.js";

  17: import { getDelay, isClickLikeOpenEvent as isClickLikeOpenEventShared } from "./useHoverShared.js";
  18: /**
  19:  * Provides hover interactions that should be attached to the floating element.
  20:  */
  21: export function useHoverFloatingInteraction(context, parameters = {}) {
  22:   const store = 'rootStore' in context ? context.rootStore : context;
  23:   const open = store.useState('open');
  24:   const floatingElement = store.useState('floatingElement');
  25:   const domReferenceElement = store.useState('domReferenceElement');
  26:   const {
  27:     dataRef
  28:   } = store.context;
  29:   const {
  30:     enabled = true,
  31:     closeDelay: closeDelayProp = 0,
  32:     nodeId: nodeIdProp
  33:   } = parameters;
  34:   const instance = useHoverInteractionSharedState(store);
  35:   const tree = useFloatingTree();
  36:   const parentId = useFloatingParentNodeId();
  37:   const isClickLikeOpenEvent = useStableCallback(() => {
  38:     return isClickLikeOpenEventShared(dataRef.current.openEvent?.type, instance.interactedInside);
  39:   });
  40:   const isHoverOpen = useStableCallback(() => {
  41:     const type = dataRef.current.openEvent?.type;
  42:     return type?.includes('mouse') && type !== 'mousedown';
  43:   });
  44:   const isRelatedTargetInsideEnabledTrigger = useStableCallback(target => {
  45:     return isTargetInsideEnabledTrigger(target, store.context.triggerElements);
  46:   });
  47:   const closeWithDelay = React.useCallback(event => {
  48:     const closeDelay = getDelay(closeDelayProp, 'close', instance.pointerType);
  49:     const close = () => {
  50:       store.setOpen(false, createChangeEventDetails(REASONS.triggerHover, event));
  51:       tree?.events.emit('floating.closed', event);
  52:     };
  53:     if (closeDelay) {
  54:       instance.openChangeTimeout.start(closeDelay, close);
  55:     } else {
  56:       instance.openChangeTimeout.clear();
  57:       close();
  58:     }
  59:   }, [closeDelayProp, store, instance, tree]);
  60:   const clearPointerEvents = useStableCallback(() => {
  61:     clearSafePolygonPointerEventsMutation(instance);
  62:   });
  63:   const handleInteractInside = useStableCallback(event => {
  64:     const target = getTarget(event);
  65:     if (!isInteractiveElement(target)) {
  66:       instance.interactedInside = false;
  67:       return;
  68:     }
  69:     instance.interactedInside = target?.closest('[aria-haspopup]') != null;
  70:   });
  71:   useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
  72:     if (!open) {
  73:       instance.pointerType = undefined;
  74:       instance.restTimeoutPending = false;
  75:       instance.interactedInside = false;
  76:       clearPointerEvents();
  77:     }
  78:   }, [open, instance, clearPointerEvents]);
  79:   React.useEffect(() => {
  80:     return clearPointerEvents;
  81:   }, [clearPointerEvents]);
  82:   useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
  83:     if (!enabled) {
  84:       return undefined;
  85:     }
  86:     if (open && instance.handleCloseOptions?.blockPointerEvents && isHoverOpen() && isElement(domReferenceElement) && floatingElement) {
  87:       const ref = domReferenceElement;
  88:       const floatingEl = floatingElement;
  89:       const doc = ownerDocument(floatingElement);
  90:       const parentFloating = tree?.nodesRef.current.find(node => node.id === parentId)?.context?.elements.floating;
  91:       if (parentFloating) {
  92:         parentFloating.style.pointerEvents = '';
  93:       }
  94:       const scopeElement = instance.handleCloseOptions?.getScope?.() ?? instance.pointerEventsScopeElement ?? parentFloating ?? ref.closest('[data-rootownerid]') ?? doc.body;
  95:       applySafePolygonPointerEventsMutation(instance, {
  96:         scopeElement,
  97:         referenceElement: ref,
  98:         floatingElement: floatingEl
  99:       });
 100:       return () => {
 101:         clearPointerEvents();
 102:       };
 103:     }
 104:     return undefined;
 105:   }, [enabled, open, domReferenceElement, floatingElement, instance, isHoverOpen, tree, parentId, clearPointerEvents]);
 106:   const childClosedTimeout = useTimeout();
 107:   React.useEffect(() => {
 108:     if (!enabled) {
 109:       return undefined;
 110:     }
 111:     function onFloatingMouseEnter() {
 112:       instance.openChangeTimeout.clear();
 113:       childClosedTimeout.clear();
 114:       tree?.events.off('floating.closed', onNodeClosed);
 115:       clearPointerEvents();
 116:     }
 117:     function onFloatingMouseLeave(event) {
 118:       if (tree && parentId && getNodeChildren(tree.nodesRef.current, parentId).length > 0) {
 119:         tree.events.on('floating.closed', onNodeClosed);
 120:         return;
 121:       }
 122:       if (isRelatedTargetInsideEnabledTrigger(event.relatedTarget)) {
 123:         // If the mouse is leaving the reference element to another trigger, don't explicitly close the popup
 124:         // as it will be moved.
 125:         return;
 126:       }
 127:       const currentNodeId = dataRef.current.floatingContext?.nodeId ?? nodeIdProp;
 128:       const relatedTarget = event.relatedTarget;
 129:       const isMovingIntoDescendantFloating = tree && currentNodeId && isElement(relatedTarget) && getNodeChildren(tree.nodesRef.current, currentNodeId, false).some(node => contains(node.context?.elements.floating, relatedTarget));
 130:       if (isMovingIntoDescendantFloating) {
 131:         return;
 132:       }
 133: 
 134:       // If the safePolygon handler is active, let it handle the close logic.
 135:       if (instance.handler) {
 136:         instance.handler(event);
 137:         return;
 138:       }
 139:       clearPointerEvents();
 140:       if (!isClickLikeOpenEvent()) {
 141:         closeWithDelay(event);
 142:       }
 143:     }
 144:     function onNodeClosed(event) {
 145:       if (!tree || !parentId || getNodeChildren(tree.nodesRef.current, parentId).length > 0) {
 146:         return;
 147:       }
 148:       // Allow the mouseenter event to fire in case child was closed because mouse moved into parent.
 149:       childClosedTimeout.start(0, () => {
 150:         tree.events.off('floating.closed', onNodeClosed);
 151:         store.setOpen(false, createChangeEventDetails(REASONS.triggerHover, event));
 152:         tree.events.emit('floating.closed', event);
 153:       });
 154:     }
 155:     const floating = floatingElement;
 156:     return mergeCleanups(floating && addEventListener(floating, 'mouseenter', onFloatingMouseEnter), floating && addEventListener(floating, 'mouseleave', onFloatingMouseLeave), floating && addEventListener(floating, 'pointerdown', handleInteractInside, true), () => {
 157:       tree?.events.off('floating.closed', onNodeClosed);
 158:     });
 159:   }, [enabled, floatingElement, store, dataRef, nodeIdProp, isClickLikeOpenEvent, isRelatedTargetInsideEnabledTrigger, closeWithDelay, clearPointerEvents, handleInteractInside, instance, tree, parentId, childClosedTimeout]);
 160: }
